# FilterTube Objective Coverage Ledger - 2026-05-18

Status: audit ledger. This is not an implementation patch.

Completion is not proven. The current state is NOT READY for implementation
changes. This ledger maps the original broad audit objective to the current
proof artifacts and the remaining gaps, so a green current-behavior harness is
not mistaken for a complete codebase audit.

## Objective Terms

The audit objective explicitly covers:

- every feature
- every file
- every method
- every JSON path
- every DOM selector
- every runtime observer/listener/timer
- every settings mode
- every cross-feature interaction
- reliability risks
- false-hide risks
- leak risks
- performance risks
- code-burden risks
- the boundary before implementation changes

The ignored root-level HTML/JSON/TXT files listed in `.gitignore` are raw
evidence inputs. They helped build `docs/json_paths_encyclopedia.md` and
`docs/youtube_renderer_inventory.md`, but they are not product source and they
are not release inputs. The only capture evidence that counts as runnable
behavior proof is a small committed fixture under
`tests/runtime/fixtures/captures/` with source-family metadata and a matching
current-behavior test.

## What Can Continue Safely

- Extract minimal fixtures from ignored root captures into
  `tests/runtime/fixtures/captures/`.
- Add instrumentation-neutral counters and contracts.
- Add source-boundary, lifecycle, selector, renderer, settings, and mutation
  proof without changing runtime decisions.
- Convert named P0 fixture obligations from
  `docs/audit/FILTERTUBE_P0_FIXTURE_GATE_REGISTER_2026-05-18.md` into runnable
  positive/negative behavior fixtures and side-effect counters.
- Continue slicing P0 fixture families into current-behavior tests like
  `tests/runtime/p0-no-work-current-behavior.test.mjs` and
  `tests/runtime/p0-endpoint-policy-current-behavior.test.mjs` before any
  runtime behavior is flipped.
- Update the readiness gate when new proof exists.

## What Remains Blocked

- Changing JSON filtering behavior.
- Deleting or broadening DOM fallback behavior.
- Changing empty whitelist or empty blocklist semantics.
- Introducing simultaneous allow/block data migration.
- Changing message sender trust behavior.
- Changing lifecycle teardown or fullscreen/native-overlay quiet behavior.
- Shipping release or website claims that are not tied to artifact proof.
